beginSubroutine: s32'DryFire'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
    ifNot: Mem(ExGauge2)
      checkInput: (INPUT_RELEASE_H)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(CPUVal2)
        storeValue: Mem(CPUVal2), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(PlayerVal7)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(0)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
          ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(100)
          endIf: 
          characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_COS_21'
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge2), Val(20)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'HoldCheck_Stand'
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg2)
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg5)
        if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
          ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
            callPrivateFunction: s32'cos_HoldGun', 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
            linkExBlendOnSprite: 0
            overwriteLinkBone: s32'weapon', s32'G_wep_grip_L', s32'body', s32'G_grip_L'
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_00'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_01'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_02'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_03'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(5)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_04'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_05'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(7)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_06'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(8)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_07'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(9)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_08'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_09'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(11)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_10'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(12)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_11'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(13)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos280_12'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
            callPrivateFunction: s32'cos_HoldGun', 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
            linkExBlendOnSprite: -1
            overwriteLinkBone: s32'weapon', s32'G_wep_grip_L', s32'body', s32'G_holster_attach_L'
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_00'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_01'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_02'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_03'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(5)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_04'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_05'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(7)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_06'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(8)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_07'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(9)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_08'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_09'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(11)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_10'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(12)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_11'
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(13)
            onSpriteChange: s32'cos000_12'
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(2)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'N_hold'
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(200)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(1000)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(101)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'N_holdend'
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(250)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(2000)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'HoldCheck_FWalk'
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
    if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
      ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
        callPrivateFunction: s32'cos_HoldGun', 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
        linkExBlendOnSprite: 0
        overwriteLinkBone: s32'weapon', s32'G_wep_grip_L', s32'body', s32'G_grip_L'
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        onSpriteChange: s32'cos285_00'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
        onSpriteChange: s32'cos285_01'

      setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(4)

beginSubroutine: s32'CheckVoiceFunc'
  returnValue: 0, 0
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bkn'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sin'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bed'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'SetGageRate'
  storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(0)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(7)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(42)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(360000)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(7)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(42)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(360000)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(420000)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(7)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(42)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(21)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(420000)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(480000)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(8)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(48)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(24)
